\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{/* Note that you may define \_\_CF\_\_KnR before \#include cfortran.h, in order to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{generate K\&R C instead of the default ANSI C. The differences are mainly in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{function prototypes and declarations. All machines, except the Apollo, work}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{with either style. The Apollo's argument promotion rules require ANSI or use of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{the obsolete std\_\$call which we have not implemented here. Hence on the Apollo,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{only C calling FORTRAN subroutines will work using K\&R style.*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l00162}00162 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01382}01382 \textcolor{comment}{/*N.B. PROTOCCALLSFFUNn(..) generates code, whether or not the FORTRAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01383}01383 \textcolor{comment}{  function is called. Therefore, especially for creator's of C header files}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01384}01384 \textcolor{comment}{  for large FORTRAN libraries which include many functions, to reduce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01385}01385 \textcolor{comment}{  compile time and object code size, it may be desirable to create}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01386}01386 \textcolor{comment}{  preprocessor directives to allow users to create code for only those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01387}01387 \textcolor{comment}{  functions which they use.                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01388}01388 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01389}01389 \textcolor{comment}{/* The following defines the maximum length string that a function can return.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01390}01390 \textcolor{comment}{   Of course it may be undefine-\/d and re-\/define-\/d before individual}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01391}01391 \textcolor{comment}{   PROTOCCALLSFFUNn(..) as required. It would also be nice to have this derived}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01392}01392 \textcolor{comment}{   from the individual machines' limits.                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01393}01393 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define MAX\_LEN\_FORTRAN\_FUNCTION\_STRING 0x4FE}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01964}01964 \textcolor{comment}{/*  N.B. Create a separate function instead of using (call function, function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01965}01965 \textcolor{comment}{value here) because in order to create the variables needed for the input}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01966}01966 \textcolor{comment}{arg.'s which may be const.'s one has to do the creation within \{\}, but these}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01967}01967 \textcolor{comment}{can never be placed within ()'s. Therefore one must create wrapper functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01968}01968 \textcolor{comment}{gcc, on the other hand may be able to avoid the wrapper functions. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01969}01969 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01970}01970 \textcolor{comment}{/* Prototypes are needed to correctly handle the value returned correctly. N.B.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01971}01971 \textcolor{comment}{Can only have prototype arg.'s with difficulty, a la G... table since FORTRAN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01972}01972 \textcolor{comment}{functions returning strings have extra arg.'s. Don't bother, since this only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01973}01973 \textcolor{comment}{causes a compiler warning to come up when one uses FCALLSCFUNn and CCALLSFFUNn}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01974}01974 \textcolor{comment}{for the same function in the same source code. Something done by the experts in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cfortran_8h_source_l01975}01975 \textcolor{comment}{debugging only.*/}    }
